10 (0) REM MATRIX MULTIPLICATION
11 (1) OPTION BASE 0
12 (1) OPTION MAX_DIM 200
20 (1) LET N = 149
21 (1) LET N1 = N + 1
22 (1) LET N2 = N1 / 2
30 (1) DIM M(N, N)
40 (1) PRINT "GENERATING MATRIX..."
42 (1) GOSUB 100
50 (1) PRINT "MULTIPLYING..."
52 (1) MAT LET M2 = M * M
60 (1) PRINT M(N2, N2)
70 (1) PRINT "INPUT MATRIX:"
72 (1) MAT PRINT M
80 (1) PRINT "OUTPUT MATRIX:"
82 (1) MAT PRINT M2
90 (1) STOP
100 (0) REM GENERATE MATRIX
110 G(110) (1) LET T = 1 / N1 / N1
120 G(110) F(I:120) (1) FOR I = 0 TO N
130 G(110) F(I:120,J:130) (150) FOR J = 0 TO N
140 G(110) F(I:120,J:130) (22500) LET M(I, J) = T * (I - J) * (I + J)
150 G(110) F(I:120,J:130) (22500) NEXT J
160 G(110) F(I:120) (150) NEXT I
190 G(110) (1) RETURN
199 (0) END
